109	def get_lower_attrib(name):
110	    # get attribute to compare against _DC_TERMS or _DC_ELEMENTS
111	    return re.sub(r".*\.", "", name).lower()
112	
113	
114	class DublinCoreExtractor:
115	    """DublinCore extractor following extruct API."""
116	
117	    def extract(self, htmlstring, base_url=None, encoding="UTF-8"):
118	        tree = parse_html(htmlstring, encoding=encoding)
119	        return list(self.extract_items(tree, base_url=base_url))
120	
121	    def extract_items(self, document, base_url=None):
122	        elements = []
123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())
128	
129	        def populate_results(node, main_attrib):
130	            # fill list with DC Elements or DC Terms
131	            node_attrib = node.attrib

109	def get_lower_attrib(name):
110	    # get attribute to compare against _DC_TERMS or _DC_ELEMENTS
111	    return re.sub(r".*\.", "", name).lower()
112	
113	
114	class DublinCoreExtractor:
115	    """DublinCore extractor following extruct API."""
116	
117	    def extract(self, htmlstring, base_url=None, encoding="UTF-8"):
118	        tree = parse_html(htmlstring, encoding=encoding)
119	        return list(self.extract_items(tree, base_url=base_url))
120	
121	    def extract_items(self, document, base_url=None):
122	        elements = []
123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())
128	
129	        def populate_results(node, main_attrib):
130	            # fill list with DC Elements or DC Terms
131	            node_attrib = node.attrib
132	            if main_attrib not in node_attrib:
133	                return
134	
135	            name = node.attrib[main_attrib]
136	            lower_name = get_lower_attrib(name)
137	            if lower_name in _DC_ELEMENTS:
138	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_ELEMENTS[lower_name]})
139	                elements.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
140	
141	            elif lower_name in _DC_TERMS:
142	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_TERMS[lower_name]})
143	                terms.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
144	
145	        namespaces_nodes = document.xpath('//link[contains(@rel,"schema")]')
146	        namespaces = {}
147	        for i in namespaces_nodes:
148	            url = strip_html5_whitespace(i.attrib["href"])
149	            if url in _URL_NAMESPACES:
150	                namespaces.update({re.sub(r"schema\.", "", i.attrib["rel"]): url})
151

123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())

106	_URL_NAMESPACES = ["http://purl.org/dc/terms/", "http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/"]
107	
108	
109	def get_lower_attrib(name):
110	    # get attribute to compare against _DC_TERMS or _DC_ELEMENTS
111	    return re.sub(r".*\.", "", name).lower()
112	
113	
114	class DublinCoreExtractor:
115	    """DublinCore extractor following extruct API."""
116	
117	    def extract(self, htmlstring, base_url=None, encoding="UTF-8"):
118	        tree = parse_html(htmlstring, encoding=encoding)
119	        return list(self.extract_items(tree, base_url=base_url))
120	
121	    def extract_items(self, document, base_url=None):
122	        elements = []
123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())
128	
129	        def populate_results(node, main_attrib):
130	            # fill list with DC Elements or DC Terms
131	            node_attrib = node.attrib
132	            if main_attrib not in node_attrib:
133	                return
134	
135	            name = node.attrib[main_attrib]
136	            lower_name = get_lower_attrib(name)
137	            if lower_name in _DC_ELEMENTS:
138	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_ELEMENTS[lower_name]})
139	                elements.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
140	
141	            elif lower_name in _DC_TERMS:
142	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_TERMS[lower_name]})
143	                terms.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
144	
145	        namespaces_nodes = document.xpath('//link[contains(@rel,"schema")]')
146	        namespaces = {}
147	        for i in namespaces_nodes:
148	            url = strip_html5_whitespace(i.attrib["href"])
149	            if url in _URL_NAMESPACES:
150	                namespaces.update({re.sub(r"schema\.", "", i.attrib["rel"]): url})
151	
152	        list_meta_node = document.xpath("//meta")
153	        for meta_node in list_meta_node:
154	            populate_results(meta_node, "name")
155	
156	        list_link_node = document.xpath("//link")
157	        for link_node in list_link_node:
158	            populate_results(link_node, "rel")
159	
160	        yield {"namespaces": namespaces, "elements": elements, "terms": terms}

138	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_ELEMENTS[lower_name]})
139	                elements.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))

108	
109	def get_lower_attrib(name):
110	    # get attribute to compare against _DC_TERMS or _DC_ELEMENTS
111	    return re.sub(r".*\.", "", name).lower()
112	
113	
114	class DublinCoreExtractor:
115	    """DublinCore extractor following extruct API."""
116	
117	    def extract(self, htmlstring, base_url=None, encoding="UTF-8"):
118	        tree = parse_html(htmlstring, encoding=encoding)
119	        return list(self.extract_items(tree, base_url=base_url))
120	
121	    def extract_items(self, document, base_url=None):
122	        elements = []
123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())
128	
129	        def populate_results(node, main_attrib):
130	            # fill list with DC Elements or DC Terms
131	            node_attrib = node.attrib
132	            if main_attrib not in node_attrib:
133	                return
134	
135	            name = node.attrib[main_attrib]
136	            lower_name = get_lower_attrib(name)
137	            if lower_name in _DC_ELEMENTS:
138	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_ELEMENTS[lower_name]})
139	                elements.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
140	
141	            elif lower_name in _DC_TERMS:
142	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_TERMS[lower_name]})
143	                terms.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
144	
145	        namespaces_nodes = document.xpath('//link[contains(@rel,"schema")]')
146	        namespaces = {}
147	        for i in namespaces_nodes:
148	            url = strip_html5_whitespace(i.attrib["href"])
149	            if url in _URL_NAMESPACES:
150	                namespaces.update({re.sub(r"schema\.", "", i.attrib["rel"]): url})
151	
152	        list_meta_node = document.xpath("//meta")
153	        for meta_node in list_meta_node:
154	            populate_results(meta_node, "name")
155	
156	        list_link_node = document.xpath("//link")
157	        for link_node in list_link_node:
158	            populate_results(link_node, "rel")
159	
160	        yield {"namespaces": namespaces, "elements": elements, "terms": terms}

148	            url = strip_html5_whitespace(i.attrib["href"])
149	            if url in _URL_NAMESPACES:
150	                namespaces.update({re.sub(r"schema\.", "", i.attrib["rel"]): url})
151	
152	        list_meta_node = document.xpath("//meta")
153	        for meta_node in list_meta_node:
154	            populate_results(meta_node, "name")
155	
156	        list_link_node = document.xpath("//link")
157	        for link_node in list_link_node:
158	            populate_results(link_node, "rel")
159	
160	        yield {"namespaces": namespaces, "elements": elements, "terms": terms}

109	def get_lower_attrib(name):
110	    # get attribute to compare against _DC_TERMS or _DC_ELEMENTS
111	    return re.sub(r".*\.", "", name).lower()

113	
114	class DublinCoreExtractor:
115	    """DublinCore extractor following extruct API."""
116	
117	    def extract(self, htmlstring, base_url=None, encoding="UTF-8"):
118	        tree = parse_html(htmlstring, encoding=encoding)
119	        return list(self.extract_items(tree, base_url=base_url))
120	
121	    def extract_items(self, document, base_url=None):
122	        elements = []
123	        terms = []
124	
125	        def attrib_to_dict(attribs):
126	            # convert _attrib type to dict
127	            return dict(attribs.items())
128	
129	        def populate_results(node, main_attrib):
130	            # fill list with DC Elements or DC Terms
131	            node_attrib = node.attrib
132	            if main_attrib not in node_attrib:
133	                return
134	
135	            name = node.attrib[main_attrib]
136	            lower_name = get_lower_attrib(name)
137	            if lower_name in _DC_ELEMENTS:
138	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_ELEMENTS[lower_name]})
139	                elements.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
140	
141	            elif lower_name in _DC_TERMS:
142	                node.attrib.update({"URI": _DC_TERMS[lower_name]})
143	                terms.append(attrib_to_dict(node.attrib))
144	
145	        namespaces_nodes = document.xpath('//link[contains(@rel,"schema")]')
146	        namespaces = {}
147	        for i in namespaces_nodes:
148	            url = strip_html5_whitespace(i.attrib["href"])
149	            if url in _URL_NAMESPACES:
150	                namespaces.update({re.sub(r"schema\.", "", i.attrib["rel"]): url})
151	
152	        list_meta_node = document.xpath("//meta")
153	        for meta_node in list_meta_node:
154	            populate_results(meta_node, "name")
155	
156	        list_link_node = document.xpath("//link")
157	        for link_node in list_link_node:
158	            populate_results(link_node, "rel")
159	
160	        yield {"namespaces": namespaces, "elements": elements, "terms": terms}
